[endif] 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav main modi lahar ke chalate upi se koi bhi muslim ummidavaar chunaav nahin jeet sakaa tha
 This was the first time since independence that no Muslim member could represent the state in the Lok Sabha
 aise main areldi kii tabassum hasan kairana upachunaav main jeet hasil karke upi kaa iklauta muslim cheharaa ban gai hai
 Please tell that this seat was vacant due to the death of Hukum Singh, BJP MP from Kairana Lok Sabha seat
 bijepi neis seat par hukum singh kii beti mriganka singh ko maidan main utaara tha
 At the same time, Tabassum Hasan was the joint candidate of opposition from RLD
 tabassum ne bijepi ummidavaar ko kareeb 50 hajaar maton se maat di he
 Tabassum Hasan won the Lok Sabha election from Kairana in 2009 as well
 tabassum saansad rah chuke akhtar hasan kii bahu or munnwar hasan kii patni hai
 The Hassan family has its own domination in the politics of Kairana
 bataa den ki upi main musalamaanon kii kareeb 19 fisadi aabaadi he
 There are 20 Lok Sabha seats in the state, where more than 20 percent are Muslims and 10 Lok Sabha seats are where more than 30 percent are Muslims
 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav main upi main samaajawaadee party ne 14, bahujan samaaj party ne 19 or congress ne nau muslim ummidavaar khadey kiye the
 Most of these seats were from Muslim dominated areas
 iske baavjood koi muslim jeetne main safal nahin ho sakaa tha
 According to political experts, it was the result of unprecedented polarization, which led to neither the dalit-muslim equation nor the muslim-yadav card
 bijepi or uske sahyogi apana dal ne ek bhi muslim ko bataur ummidavaar tikat nahin diya tha
 In 2014, the BJP alliance got 73 seats from 80 seats in UP
 gauratlab he ki 2014 caloksabhaa chunaavamein desh bhar se kul 22 muslim saansad hi jeet sake the
 This figure was the lowest
 2009 kii loksabhaa kii baat karen to isamen kul 30 musalmaan saansad the
 The best figure for Muslim representation was in 1980 when there were a total of 49 Muslim mps in the Lok Sabha
 aam taur par loksabhaa main muslim pratinidhitiv kaa aankada 25 se 30 ke bich hi rahata he
 BJP candidates from Kaithal have forgotten their election symbol and have been in the INLD before the appeal of the button to press the button on the INLD mark
 kahin prachaar ke tareeke charchaa kaa vishay banate hai to kabhi netaaon ke bayaan surkhiyaan batorte hai
 One such incident has been seen in Haryana, where the Bharatiya Janata Party candidate appealed to the public to press the button on the election symbol of another party
 yah dilachasp vakya kaithal kaa he
 From here, BJP has given ticket to Lilaram Gurjar
 chunaav prachaar charam par he or leelaram bhi isi kadi main janata ke bich vot maangane pahunche the
 But while appealing for the vote, he forgot his own sign
 leelaram ne janata se bijepi kii bajaayanintha ke chunaav chinh par muharlagane kii apil kar daali
 The atmosphere of the meeting changed on Lilaram's statement The atmosphere of the meeting changed after hearing this statement of Lilaram
 log hansi-majaak karne lage
 Soon Lilaram Gurjar realized that he had made a mistake and corrected it
 bataa den ki ki leelaram gurjar kii shuruaati raajnneeti INLD se judi rahi he
 He has also contested on INLD (INLD) ticket from Kaithal seat
 2014 main wo bijepi main aae
 Assembly elections are being held for 90 seats in Haryana
 yahaan 21 oktober ko matdaan hoga, jabaki maton kii gananaa 24 oktober ko hogi
 Buildings in the capital Santiago were shaken due to a severe earthquake in central Chile, but there was no immediate casualty or heavy damage
 yues jiyological survey ne khabar di he ki is bukamp kii tivrata 6
 It was rated 6 and its center was at a depth of 10 kilometers (six miles) to the southwest, about 65 kilometers (40 mi) from the town of Coquimbo
